, &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">GRAND FATHER OF RABINDRANATH TAGORE</span> , THE NOBEL PRIZE WINNER</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-1n7slPjv72c/TkvoRQb9_0I/AAAAAAAAFZY/9jR46Rv4zyU/s1600/2676599070104237032S600x600Q85.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-1n7slPjv72c/TkvoRQb9_0I/AAAAAAAAFZY/9jR46Rv4zyU/s1600/2676599070104237032S600x600Q85.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Two Opium drug runners embezzled from Rothschild\u2019s East India company. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Both though that they could hoodwink vicious Rothschild in the drug business. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Both were invited to Britain ostensibly to be honored in England and France by the Royalty. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Both were secretly slow poisoned to death, after the bulk of the money these thieves looted&nbsp;was retrieved back, and they had served their purpose <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>\u2014 one in 1833 and the other in 1846. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Both are buried in Britain. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LXAy2YpXzkM/TkvooyJLxZI/AAAAAAAAFZc/4Ed2r7UvqUg/s1600/Raja_Ram_Mohan_Roy.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LXAy2YpXzkM/TkvooyJLxZI/AAAAAAAAFZc/4Ed2r7UvqUg/s1600/Raja_Ram_Mohan_Roy.jpg\" width=\"242\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The first to go was Raja Ram Mohan Roy, and the next to go was Dwarkanath Tagore , on 1<sup>st</sup> Aug 1846 at St George\u2019s hotel in London. </span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dwarkanath was the grandfather of Rabindranath Tagore, the Nobel prize winner. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Rabindranath never wrote about his grandfather and he made sure all dubious documents related to him were destroyed in India.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Both Ram Mohan Roy and Dwarkanath Tagore are buried in Britain.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">See pictures below.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; Considerable material is available in&nbsp; US universities, of the Opium activities of the Bengali Brown Sahibs.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-kY32UFTZ35I/TkvqwYQ5cuI/AAAAAAAAFaQ/_Pb-6gwPvFA/s1600/WDB.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Let me quote Wikipedia:<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">QUOTE - G. D. Birla's\nfather, Baldeodas Birla, was adopted from the Navalgarh Birla family.\nBaldeodas's fortune was made in partnership with his nephew, Fulchand Sodhani,\nthrough speculation in the opium trade running into more than 10 million\nrupees, in which his elder brother Jugal Kishore Birla had earned a name-UNQUOTE</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-h0JSMfu8V44/TkvpRfsdLbI/AAAAAAAAFZ0/TGXStlo09LM/s1600/imagesCANKI0C0.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"365\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-h0JSMfu8V44/TkvpRfsdLbI/AAAAAAAAFZ0/TGXStlo09LM/s1600/imagesCANKI0C0.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The drug running Parsees left their trail with Jardine and Matheson offices in Hong Kong. Those days you hide secret documents in dark places , and then forget where you placed them. </span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-r5ItSePB4ss/TkvpEwOmAuI/AAAAAAAAFZs/cuqrZ8uCQPA/s1600/2902768250104237032S600x600Q85.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-r5ItSePB4ss/TkvpEwOmAuI/AAAAAAAAFZs/cuqrZ8uCQPA/s1600/2902768250104237032S600x600Q85.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">In this post I will speak only of <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>Dwarkanath Tagore- the </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">fabulously&nbsp;rich grandfather of Rabindranath Tagore</span>.</span> <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ghansham Birla did NOT have his own ships.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">But Dwarkanath had his own fleet of small and big clipper ships. His smaller clippers SS Ariel and SS Mavis did the drug running routes from Hoogly river and Chalna - Chitttagong rivers, making 2500 % middleman profits. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Ffg35oFurkU/TkvpW_LzPRI/AAAAAAAAFZ4/ej0HDoF7m6M/s1600/imagesCA89TUOR.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Ffg35oFurkU/TkvpW_LzPRI/AAAAAAAAFZ4/ej0HDoF7m6M/s1600/imagesCA89TUOR.jpg\" width=\"268\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dwarkanath even bought himself a big ship SS India on which he travelled to London in style to meet Queen Victoria in Jan 1842.&nbsp;&nbsp; When he arrived at London, the entire British royalty including Queen Victoria , plus&nbsp;Prime Minister Sir Robert Peel and the Rothschild clan was at the gangway to receive him. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Rothschild even forced busy Charles Dickens to dine with brown sahib Dwarkanath.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Rothschild got Dwarkanath&nbsp;invited to Paris by the French King Louise Phillipe who came all the way to St Clauden to receive him in Oct 1842.. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Why not? font-size: large;\">Cant put too many words in this mushy post-- </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Qvp46TG1v9E/TkpZFRPilaI/AAAAAAAAFXw/QLOrqQheigQ/s1600/imagesCAW3XB4Y.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">The old Alumni meet of Kendriya Vidyalaya No1 , Calicut on 14th August 2011</span> ,  <span style=\"color: blue;\">(<em> </em></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><em><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: blue;\">fir</span><span style=\"color: blue;\">st</span> <span style=\"color: blue;\">at 0900 AM for a regular kids type morning assembly at school and then for a evening bash at Calicut Towers</span></span></em> </span>) was truly a nostalgic affair -- </span></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: Times; font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: black;\">-- rather one of quantum reminiscence.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-vUI3fLp6ylw/TkpZYqNNFPI/AAAAAAAAFX4/dKIk2JZusSg/s1600/imagesCA62V8M6.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TvkqKSLpoew/TktjljWjqqI/AAAAAAAAFZM/G-uy-nEqy3U/s1600/imagesCATQH98Z.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TvkqKSLpoew/TktjljWjqqI/AAAAAAAAFZM/G-uy-nEqy3U/s400/imagesCATQH98Z.jpg\" height=\"400\" width=\"285\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nChanting the assembly prayer ASTO MA SADH GAMAYA &nbsp;after nearly 4 decades -- could not believe it was all lodged firmly in my sub-conscious. It flowed out like a river.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-u-2FEQIBHp0/TkngPqMqAMI/AAAAAAAAFWg/scHOGbIcyEQ/s1600/295069_10150337188464524_710234523_9817675_5895959_n.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">Ephemeral disjointed memories resurrected to their colourful old splendour.&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">Some of us were meeting after 4 decades.&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">It was magic weaving time, and this hardcore sailor felt truly vulnerable after a very long time.  </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-q5cb5tvulUg/Tkp1Ai0dI0I/AAAAAAAAFYQ/4J47GO9oeHc/s1600/imagesCAERY2KD.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">What with my subconscious spewing like mad -- </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">quantum waves of presence swirling around waves of loss-- </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">my consciousness collapsing them for yet another one to rise --- </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">sentiments and remembrance tumbling over each other like crazy -- </span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">so much of clean bacchanalia -- leg pullin' , reminding each other of our first crushes and loves --&nbsp;unadulterated fun--</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: Times; font-size: large;\">my emotional chords doing the sweet twang all the while --   </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-NNfT448_V2s/TkpZQ0bpELI/AAAAAAAAFX0/7Zersjb86ZA/s1600/up.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-d6OJdb-nXck/TklAYV3id1I/AAAAAAAAFWY/FTpa6oXD25c/s1600/untitled.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-d6OJdb-nXck/TklAYV3id1I/AAAAAAAAFWY/FTpa6oXD25c/s400/untitled.png\" height=\"400\" width=\"300\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><br />\n</span><span style=\"color: black;\"> </span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-size: large;\">--and then old student and national singer Chitra Iyer with her killer eyes ,went on stage  , and belted out the soulful Lagja Gale Laga -- </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-size: large;\">and sprayed such sweet sorrow on us -- </span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-size: x-large;\">Jeez!!&nbsp; </span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: black; font-size: x-large;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Love is powerful enough, but if you mix it with nostalgia , it becomes too potent and gives you a dull pain on the&nbsp;left hand side of your chest.</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\nIn the seventies, our school used to take the prize for all Inter school competitions, be brawn or brain. <br />\n<br />\nI met two girls and when we reminisced , we realised that in the group photo with the trophy which came in the 1970 newspaper ( our school had won the district inter-school athletic championship at Mananchira maidan ) both were sitting right in front of me. My contribution was&nbsp;a modest bronze in the 200 metres race.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SfeBSCBTDU0/TkspPXsCaMI/AAAAAAAAFZE/lBqL0r4xBzg/s1600/imagesCA84K74J.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-SfeBSCBTDU0/TkspPXsCaMI/AAAAAAAAFZE/lBqL0r4xBzg/s1600/imagesCA84K74J.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nI felt sad to see my childhood hero, MV Prakash sitting quietly in a corner, away from the limelight. &nbsp;A lot was said that day about famous brother / sister combinations, in the quiz programme. &nbsp;Well what do they know?&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nLet me put on record via this post, that none can come anywhere near the Prakash/ Devprasad/ Srilata combination on the nineteen sixtees. The trio would come to school in a open Jeep with one of the brothers driving.<br />\n<br />\nPrakash was the hero of Calicut, NOT just of our school, as his pole vault records were unsurpassed for many years.&nbsp; He would NOT compete in the heats and would say \"pass\" every time the bar was raised -- and when all the also-rans had fallen by the wayside, he would give that final Sergei Bubka vault, to set a new meet record.&nbsp; He used to be quite humble about the whole thing. And everybody knew he would do it.&nbsp; No hype, no hooplah, no victory laps.&nbsp; Devprasad , always smiling, was the Carl&nbsp;Lewis of our school.&nbsp; And Srilata was so shy-- she is still the same.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Tz6Bns1XpIs/Tk0ZI8-vUMI/AAAAAAAAFbk/r3-CsoOJyFI/s1600/awer.png\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-Tz6Bns1XpIs/Tk0ZI8-vUMI/AAAAAAAAFbk/r3-CsoOJyFI/s400/awer.png\" height=\"271\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nIn the annual day celebrations, Principal OP Gupta would want a&nbsp;Kalari sword fight between the brothers Prakash and Devprasad. It was a indeed a terrific sight to see clanging swords and scattering sparks --<br />\n<br />\n-- memories become alive , when you step back in time.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Do these naive \" frogs in the well \"&nbsp; know the gruesome history of Calicut Free Mason lodge, when the white man held session ?&nbsp;&nbsp; This 125 years old lodge was near St Joseph's school, Calicut.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Do they even know who NIMROD is?</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">How naive can you get?</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Freemasons give an official response in their web sites as follows--</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;lucida sans unicode&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><em><span style=\"color: blue;\">Freemasonry is a fraternal organisation firmly entrenched in tradition and history. The original Constitutions were published in 1723 and are fundamentally what all Freemasons all over the world are united by and adhere to. To change these Constitutions to allow women to become members would require Lodges throughout the world to agree to the change. As cultures are so diverse and vary so dramatically in terms of social structure and gender relations, making this fundamental change to the Constitutions would be extremely difficult</span></em>--BLAH BLAH</span></span><br />\n<br />\nOK, we got it-- it ain't no sorority,&nbsp;&nbsp; it's a fraternity--<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: #333333; font-family: &quot;lucida sans unicode&quot; , &quot;sans-serif&quot;; line-height: 115%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Let me quote ( I usually do NOT care for such third party references ) of the parallels between the Orphic path and the yogic as written by Joseph John Campbell :&nbsp;&nbsp;\u201ca system both of thought and practice, exactly paralleling that of Indian asceticism, was communicated by initiated masters to little circles of devotees.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The soul, it was declared, returned repeatedly to life, bound to the wheel of rebirth (compare the Sanskrit samsara).&nbsp;&nbsp;Through asceticism (Sanskrit, tapas), however, the body could be purged of its Titan dross (Sanskrit, mirjara, \u2018shedding\u2019) and the soul released (Sanskrit, moksha, \u2018release\u2019).&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Also, rituals fostering meditation on the godly factor were of help (Sanskrit, bhakti, \u2018devotion\u2019).&nbsp;&nbsp;And when, at last, in rapture (samadhi), the initiate cleaved to his own intrinsic being (svasvarupman), he was divine (Shivaham, \u2018I am Shiva.\u2019)\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The gay side kick of Aristotle wrote : \u201c Orpheus so hated women he chose to be reborn as a motherless swan\u201d&nbsp;&nbsp;.&nbsp;&nbsp;It is a pity that he visited India , yet he knew nothing of Brahmacharya.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">However Plato respects Orpheus for his poetry ,the sweet hymns&nbsp;&nbsp;of the hexameter form that revolutionized Greek poetry.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For Greek / Latin classics Homer's Iliad and Odyssey and Virgil's Aeneid have inherent the Dactylic hexameter ( heroic hexameter)&nbsp;&nbsp;a form of meter in poetry or a rhythmic scheme, like the metered Sanskrit verses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The mysterious The Testament of Orpheus was the most important Orphic document for six centuries after it\u2019s \u201cdiscovery\u201d circa 300 AD.&nbsp;&nbsp;In it Orpheus says when in Egypt he met Moses who taught him about monotheism.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A circa 350 AD hematite magic amulet, once in the collection of the Berlin Museum, depicted a man crucified on a cross with a moon and seven stars above his head and the words Orpheoc Bakkikoc.&nbsp;&nbsp;It was declared to be a forgery by a furious pope Pius XII.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The Orphic doctrine was purely vedic Indian and&nbsp;&nbsp;remained on a mythological plane, interpreting the universe in terms of personalized deities and procreation. Pythagoras refined and rationalized it and grabbed the glory later.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A Indian Christian trader named Theophilos, from originally from Kerala and resident in Socotra island ( Aloe vera trade ) undertook several missionary journeys on behalf of the Roman emperor Constantius in the mid-4th century.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;He writes of a small Christian community in on the Malabar coast which traces its origins to Jesus' disciples Thomas and&nbsp;&nbsp;Bartholomew.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Bartholomew is one of the 12 disciples of Jesus and ismentioned in three Synoptic gospels: Matthew,[10:1\u20134] Mark,[3:13\u201319] and Luke,[6:12\u201316] and also appears as one of the witnesses of the Ascension[Acts 1:4,12,13]; however, each time he is named in the company of Philip.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">He is not mentioned in Gospel of John.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In the mid-6th century the Alexandrian merchant Kosmas Indikopleustes (India-navigator- TEE HEEEE ) is reputed to have visited the Malabar coast and Ceylon.&nbsp;&nbsp;Kosmas was the author of a stolen world-geography and a book on stolen Kerala astronomy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In his letter The Orphic Comparison of the Sun to God Ficino explains \u201cIt is certainly in the Sun that visible light is created from the light of consciousness, and there also sight is created from&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">understanding.&nbsp;&nbsp;For there understanding is no different from the light of consciousness, nor sight from visible light.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Consciousness ?&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">TEEE HEEEE !<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;
